Curated information about every package on Nix!

nixpkgs / glimpse - Glimpse is an open source image editor based on the GNU Image Manipulation Program (GIMP). The goal is to experiment with new ideas and expand the use of free software.

Homepage - https://glimpse-editor.org

License - GPL-3.0-or-later

Maintainers - ash lea - Kerstin Humm
